***parasiet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasiet</a> (12279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasite.html>parasite</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">parasitus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράσιτος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parásitos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 16th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> “parasitic organism” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic <a href = vnd.unilang:loan.html>loan</a></a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasite.html>parasite</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasiet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasieten.html>parasieten</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:parasite.html>parasite</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">parasitic <a href = vnd.unilang:organism.html>organism</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> 19th <a href = vnd.unilang:c.html>c</a>.]</span>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">parfumer</i>.

</p>

<p>1780, <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nenets_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Nenets languages">Tundra Nenets</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="yrk">парка</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleut_language" class="extiw" title="w:Aleut language">Aleut</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ale"><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́рка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">párka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:perhaps.html>Perhaps</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic">Proto-Uralic</a></span>;
